data-pagefind-body=""><div class="hidden sm:block relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 "><nav aria-label="Breadcrumb" class="py-4 max-w-4xl md:px-4 mb-2"><ol class="flex items-center text-sm"><li><a class="hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/sql-reference">Home</a></li><li class="flex items-center"><span class="mx-2 text-v-text-3">/</span><a class="hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/sql-reference/functions">Functions</a></li><li class="flex items-center"><span class="mx-2 text-v-text-3">/</span><span class="font-semibold">Window functions</span></li></ol></nav></div><div class="relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 xl:grid xl:grid-cols-[1fr_280px]"><div class="max-w-4xl text-body md:px-4 md:pb-20 relative" role="main"><article><div class="flex flex-col sm:flex-row sm:items-center justify-between gap-4 mb-6"><h1 id="window-functions" class="t-h3" data-pagefind-weight="20.0">Window functions<a class="headerlink" href="#window-functions" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h1><div class="flex-shrink-0 w-auto"><div class="relative inline-block w-auto" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><div class="flex rounded-md overflow-hidden border border-v-border-02 hover:border-v-border-03 transition-colors"><button class="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 text-sm transition-colors min-w-[106px] text-v-text-01"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="w-4 h-4 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]"><path d="M14 2H6a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v16a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h12a2 2 0 0 0 2-2V8z"></path><path d="M14 2v6h6M16 13H8M16 17H8M10 9H8"></path></svg><span>Copy as MD</span></button><button class="flex items-center justify-center px-2 py-1.5 text-sm text-v-text-01 border-l border-v-border-02 min-w-[32px]" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" class="w-3 h-3 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]" style="margin-top:-4px;margin-left:-4px"><path fill="currentColor" d="M8.1 11.41 4 6.995 4.745 6 8.1 9.795 11.454 6l.746.994z"></path></svg></button></div></div></div></div><p>Window functions perform calculations across a set of table rows that are somehow related to the current row. They are often used for ranking, aggregating, and calculating running totals.</p><h2 id="dense-rank" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">dense_rank<a class="headerlink" href="#dense-rank" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Ranks the current row within its partition without gaps. In other words, if the value of any new row encountered is equal to the value of one of the previous rows then it will receive the next successive rank without any gaps in ranking.</p><p>The rank function provides the same behaviour, but with gaps in ranking.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Alias: <code>denseRank</code> (case-sensitive)</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">dense_rank (column_name)
  OVER ([[PARTITION BY grouping_column] [ORDER BY sorting_column]
        [ROWS or RANGE expression_to_bound_rows_withing_the_group]] | [window_name])
FROM table_name
WINDOW window_name as ([[PARTITION BY grouping_column] [ORDER BY sorting_column])
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>For more detail on window function syntax see: Window Functions - Syntax.</p><h3 id="returned-value" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returned value<a class="headerlink" href="#returned-value" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li>A number for the current row within its partition, without gaps in ranking. UInt64.</li></ul><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The following example is based on the example provided in the video instructional Ranking window functions in Tinybird.</p><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT player, salary,
       dense_rank() OVER (ORDER BY salary DESC) AS dense_rank
FROM (
  select c1::String as team, c2::String as player, c3::UInt32 as salary, c4::String as position from values (
      (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Gary Chen&#x27;, 195000, &#x27;F&#x27;),
      (&#x27;New Coreystad Archdukes&#x27;, &#x27;Charles Juarez&#x27;, 190000, &#x27;F&#x27;),
      (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Michael Stanley&#x27;, 150000, &#x27;D&#x27;),
      (&#x27;New Coreystad Archdukes&#x27;, &#x27;Scott Harrison&#x27;, 150000, &#x27;D&#x27;),
      (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Robert George&#x27;, 195000, &#x27;M&#x27;),
      (&#x27;South Hampton Seagulls&#x27;, &#x27;Douglas Benson&#x27;, 150000, &#x27;M&#x27;),
      (&#x27;South Hampton Seagulls&#x27;, &#x27;James Henderson&#x27;, 140000, &#x27;M&#x27;)
  )
)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─player──────────┬─salary─┬─dense_rank─┐
│ Gary Chen       │ 195000 │          1 │
│ Robert George   │ 195000 │          1 │
│ Charles Juarez  │ 190000 │          2 │
│ Michael Stanley │ 150000 │          3 │
│ Douglas Benson  │ 150000 │          3 │
│ Scott Harrison  │ 150000 │          3 │
│ James Henderson │ 140000 │          4 │
└─────────────────┴────────┴────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="first-value" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">first_value<a class="headerlink" href="#first-value" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Returns the first value evaluated within its ordered frame. By default, NULL arguments are skipped, however the <code>RESPECT NULLS</code> modifier can be used to override this behaviour.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">first_value (column_name) [[RESPECT NULLS] | [IGNORE NULLS]]
  OVER ([[PARTITION BY grouping_column] [ORDER BY sorting_column]
        [ROWS or RANGE expression_to_bound_rows_withing_the_group]] | [window_name])
FROM table_name
WINDOW window_name as ([PARTITION BY grouping_column] [ORDER BY sorting_column])
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Alias: <code>any</code>.</p><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>Using the optional modifier <code>RESPECT NULLS</code> after <code>first_value(column_name)</code> will ensure that <code>NULL</code> arguments aren&#x27;t skipped.</p><p>Alias: <code>first_value_respect_nulls</code></p></div></div><p>For more detail on window function syntax see: Window Functions - Syntax.</p><h3 id="returned-value" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returned value<a class="headerlink" href="#returned-value" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li>The first value evaluated within its ordered frame.</li></ul><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>In this example the <code>first_value</code> function is used to find the highest paid footballer from a fictional dataset of salaries of Premier League football players.</p><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT player, salary,
       first_value(player) OVER (ORDER BY salary DESC) AS highest_paid_player
FROM (
  select c1::String as team, c2::String as player, c3::UInt32 as salary, c4::String as position from values (
      (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Gary Chen&#x27;, 195000, &#x27;F&#x27;),
      (&#x27;New Coreystad Archdukes&#x27;, &#x27;Charles Juarez&#x27;, 190000, &#x27;F&#x27;),
      (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Michael Stanley&#x27;, 150000, &#x27;D&#x27;),
      (&#x27;New Coreystad Archdukes&#x27;, &#x27;Scott Harrison&#x27;, 150000, &#x27;D&#x27;),
      (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Robert George&#x27;, 195000, &#x27;M&#x27;),
      (&#x27;South Hampton Seagulls&#x27;, &#x27;Douglas Benson&#x27;, 150000, &#x27;M&#x27;),
      (&#x27;South Hampton Seagulls&#x27;, &#x27;James Henderson&#x27;, 140000, &#x27;M&#x27;)
  )
)

</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─player──────────┬─salary─┬─highest_paid_player─┐
│ Gary Chen       │ 196000 │ Gary Chen           │
│ Robert George   │ 195000 │ Gary Chen           │
│ Charles Juarez  │ 190000 │ Gary Chen           │
│ Scott Harrison  │ 180000 │ Gary Chen           │
│ Douglas Benson  │ 150000 │ Gary Chen           │
│ James Henderson │ 140000 │ Gary Chen           │
│ Michael Stanley │ 100000 │ Gary Chen           │
└─────────────────┴────────┴─────────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="laginframe" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">lagInFrame<a class="headerlink" href="#laginframe" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Returns a value evaluated at the row that is at a specified physical offset row before the current row within the ordered frame.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">lagInFrame(x[, offset[, default]])
  OVER ([[PARTITION BY grouping_column] [ORDER BY sorting_column]
        [ROWS or RANGE expression_to_bound_rows_withing_the_group]] | [window_name])
FROM table_name
WINDOW window_name as ([[PARTITION BY grouping_column] [ORDER BY sorting_column])
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>For more detail on window function syntax see: Window Functions - Syntax.</p><h3 id="parameters" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Parameters<a class="headerlink" href="#parameters" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>x</code>: Column name.</li><li><code>offset</code>: Offset to apply. (U)Int*. (Optional - <code>1</code> by default).</li><li><code>default</code>: Value to return if calculated row exceeds the boundaries of the window frame. (Optional - default value of column type when omitted).</li></ul><h3 id="returned-value" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returned value<a class="headerlink" href="#returned-value" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li>Value evaluated at the row that is at a specified physical offset before the current row within the ordered frame.</li></ul><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>This example looks at historical data for a specific stock and uses the <code>lagInFrame</code> function to calculate a day-to-day delta and percentage change in the closing price of the stock.</p><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    date,
    close,
    lagInFrame(close, 1, close) OVER (ORDER BY date ASC) AS previous_day_close,
    COALESCE(ROUND(close - previous_day_close, 2)) AS delta,
    COALESCE(ROUND((delta / previous_day_close) * 100, 2)) AS percent_change
FROM (
    select c1::Date as date, c2::Float32 as open, c3::Float32 as high, c4::Float32 as low, c5::Float32 as close, c6::UInt32 as volume from values (
    (&#x27;2024-06-03&#x27;, 113.62, 115.00, 112.00, 115.00, 438392000),
    (&#x27;2024-06-04&#x27;, 115.72, 116.60, 114.04, 116.44, 403324000),
    (&#x27;2024-06-05&#x27;, 118.37, 122.45, 117.47, 122.44, 528402000),
    (&#x27;2024-06-06&#x27;, 124.05, 125.59, 118.32, 121.00, 664696000),
    (&#x27;2024-06-07&#x27;, 119.77, 121.69, 118.02, 120.89, 412386000)
    )
)
ORDER BY date DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌───────date─┬──close─┬─previous_day_close─┬─delta─┬─percent_change─┐
│ 2024-06-07 │ 120.89 │                121 │ -0.11 │          -0.09 │
│ 2024-06-06 │    121 │             122.44 │ -1.44 │          -1.18 │
│ 2024-06-05 │ 122.44 │             116.44 │     6 │           5.15 │
│ 2024-06-04 │ 116.44 │                115 │  1.44 │           1.25 │
│ 2024-06-03 │    115 │                115 │     0 │              0 │
└────────────┴────────┴────────────────────┴───────┴────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="last-value" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">last_value<a class="headerlink" href="#last-value" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Returns the last value evaluated within its ordered frame. By default, NULL arguments are skipped, however the <code>RESPECT NULLS</code> modifier can be used to override this behaviour.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">last_value (column_name) [[RESPECT NULLS] | [IGNORE NULLS]]
  OVER ([[PARTITION BY grouping_column] [ORDER BY sorting_column]
        [ROWS or RANGE expression_to_bound_rows_withing_the_group]] | [window_name])
FROM table_name
WINDOW window_name as ([[PARTITION BY grouping_column] [ORDER BY sorting_column])
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Alias: <code>anyLast</code>.</p><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>Using the optional modifier <code>RESPECT NULLS</code> after <code>first_value(column_name)</code> will ensure that <code>NULL</code> arguments aren&#x27;t skipped.</p><p>Alias: <code>lastValueRespectNulls</code></p></div></div><p>For more detail on window function syntax see: Window Functions - Syntax.</p><h3 id="returned-value" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returned value<a class="headerlink" href="#returned-value" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li>The last value evaluated within its ordered frame.</li></ul><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>In this example the <code>last_value</code> function is used to find the lowest paid footballer from a fictional dataset of salaries of Premier League football players.</p><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT player, salary,
       last_value(player) OVER (ORDER BY salary DESC RANGE BETWEEN UNBOUNDED PRECEDING AND UNBOUNDED FOLLOWING) AS lowest_paid_player
FROM (
  select c1::String as team, c2::String as player, c3::UInt32 as salary, c4::String as position from values (
    (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Gary Chen&#x27;, 196000, &#x27;F&#x27;),
    (&#x27;New Coreystad Archdukes&#x27;, &#x27;Charles Juarez&#x27;, 190000, &#x27;F&#x27;),
    (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Michael Stanley&#x27;, 100000, &#x27;D&#x27;),
    (&#x27;New Coreystad Archdukes&#x27;, &#x27;Scott Harrison&#x27;, 180000, &#x27;D&#x27;),
    (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Robert George&#x27;, 195000, &#x27;M&#x27;),
    (&#x27;South Hampton Seagulls&#x27;, &#x27;Douglas Benson&#x27;, 150000, &#x27;M&#x27;),
    (&#x27;South Hampton Seagulls&#x27;, &#x27;James Henderson&#x27;, 140000, &#x27;M&#x27;)
  )
)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─player──────────┬─salary─┬─lowest_paid_player─┐
│ Gary Chen       │ 196000 │ Michael Stanley    │
│ Robert George   │ 195000 │ Michael Stanley    │
│ Charles Juarez  │ 190000 │ Michael Stanley    │
│ Scott Harrison  │ 180000 │ Michael Stanley    │
│ Douglas Benson  │ 150000 │ Michael Stanley    │
│ James Henderson │ 140000 │ Michael Stanley    │
│ Michael Stanley │ 100000 │ Michael Stanley    │
└─────────────────┴────────┴────────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="leadinframe" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">leadInFrame<a class="headerlink" href="#leadinframe" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Returns a value evaluated at the row that is offset rows after the current row within the ordered frame.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">leadInFrame(x[, offset[, default]])
  OVER ([[PARTITION BY grouping_column] [ORDER BY sorting_column]
        [ROWS or RANGE expression_to_bound_rows_withing_the_group]] | [window_name])
FROM table_name
WINDOW window_name as ([[PARTITION BY grouping_column] [ORDER BY sorting_column])
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>For more detail on window function syntax see: Window Functions - Syntax.</p><h3 id="parameters" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Parameters<a class="headerlink" href="#parameters" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>x</code>: Column name.</li><li><code>offset</code>: Offset to apply. (U)Int*. (Optional - <code>1</code> by default).</li><li><code>default</code>: Value to return if calculated row exceeds the boundaries of the window frame. (Optional - default value of column type when omitted).</li></ul><h3 id="returned-value" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returned value<a class="headerlink" href="#returned-value" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li>value evaluated at the row that is offset rows after the current row within the ordered frame.</li></ul><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    n,
    m,
    leadInFrame(m) OVER (
        PARTITION BY n ORDER BY m ASC ROWS BETWEEN UNBOUNDED PRECEDING AND UNBOUNDED FOLLOWING
    ) AS next
FROM
    (
        select (number % 12) + 1 n, toStartOfMonth(today()) - INTERVAL number MONTH m
        from numbers(36)
        order by m
    )
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">--------------------------------
|  n | m          | next       |
--------------------------------
|  1 | 2022-12-01 | 2023-12-01 |
|  1 | 2023-12-01 | 2024-12-01 |
|  1 | 2024-12-01 | 1970-01-01 |
|  2 | 2022-11-01 | 2023-11-01 |
|  2 | 2023-11-01 | 2024-11-01 |
|  2 | 2024-11-01 | 1970-01-01 |
|  3 | 2022-10-01 | 2023-10-01 |
|  3 | 2023-10-01 | 2024-10-01 |
|  3 | 2024-10-01 | 1970-01-01 |
|  4 | 2022-09-01 | 2023-09-01 |
|  4 | 2023-09-01 | 2024-09-01 |
|  4 | 2024-09-01 | 1970-01-01 |
|  5 | 2022-08-01 | 2023-08-01 |
|  5 | 2023-08-01 | 2024-08-01 |
|  5 | 2024-08-01 | 1970-01-01 |
|  6 | 2022-07-01 | 2023-07-01 |
|  6 | 2023-07-01 | 2024-07-01 |
|  6 | 2024-07-01 | 1970-01-01 |
|  7 | 2022-06-01 | 2023-06-01 |
|  7 | 2023-06-01 | 2024-06-01 |
|  7 | 2024-06-01 | 1970-01-01 |

| 10 | 2023-03-01 | 2024-03-01 |
| 10 | 2024-03-01 | 1970-01-01 |
| 11 | 2022-02-01 | 2023-02-01 |
| 11 | 2023-02-01 | 2024-02-01 |
| 11 | 2024-02-01 | 1970-01-01 |
| 12 | 2022-01-01 | 2023-01-01 |
| 12 | 2023-01-01 | 2024-01-01 |
| 12 | 2024-01-01 | 1970-01-01 |
--------------------------------
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="nth-value" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">nth_value<a class="headerlink" href="#nth-value" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Returns the first non-NULL value evaluated against the nth row (offset) in its ordered frame.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">nth_value (x, offset)
  OVER ([[PARTITION BY grouping_column] [ORDER BY sorting_column]
        [ROWS or RANGE expression_to_bound_rows_withing_the_group]] | [window_name])
FROM table_name
WINDOW window_name as ([[PARTITION BY grouping_column] [ORDER BY sorting_column])
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>For more detail on window function syntax see: Window Functions - Syntax.</p><h3 id="parameters" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Parameters<a class="headerlink" href="#parameters" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>x</code>: Column name.</li><li><code>offset</code>: nth row to evaluate current row against.</li></ul><h3 id="returned-value" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returned value<a class="headerlink" href="#returned-value" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li>The first non-NULL value evaluated against the nth row (offset) in its ordered frame.</li></ul><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>In this example the <code>nth-value</code> function is used to find the third-highest salary from a fictional dataset of salaries of Premier League football players.</p><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT player, salary, nth_value(player,3) OVER(ORDER BY salary DESC) AS third_highest_salary FROM
(
    select c1::String as team, c2::String as player, c3::UInt32 as salary, c4::String as position from values (
        (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Gary Chen&#x27;, 195000, &#x27;F&#x27;),
        (&#x27;New Coreystad Archdukes&#x27;, &#x27;Charles Juarez&#x27;, 190000, &#x27;F&#x27;),
        (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Michael Stanley&#x27;, 100000, &#x27;D&#x27;),
        (&#x27;New Coreystad Archdukes&#x27;, &#x27;Scott Harrison&#x27;, 180000, &#x27;D&#x27;),
        (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Robert George&#x27;, 195000, &#x27;M&#x27;),
        (&#x27;South Hampton Seagulls&#x27;, &#x27;Douglas Benson&#x27;, 150000, &#x27;M&#x27;),
        (&#x27;South Hampton Seagulls&#x27;, &#x27;James Henderson&#x27;, 140000, &#x27;M&#x27;)
    )
)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─player──────────┬─salary─┬─third_highest_salary─┐
│ Gary Chen       │ 195000 │                      │
│ Robert George   │ 195000 │                      │
│ Charles Juarez  │ 190000 │ Charles Juarez       │
│ Scott Harrison  │ 180000 │ Charles Juarez       │
│ Douglas Benson  │ 150000 │ Charles Juarez       │
│ James Henderson │ 140000 │ Charles Juarez       │
│ Michael Stanley │ 100000 │ Charles Juarez       │
└─────────────────┴────────┴──────────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="percent-rank" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">percent_rank<a class="headerlink" href="#percent-rank" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>returns the relative rank (i.e. percentile) of rows within a window partition.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Alias: <code>percentRank</code> (case-sensitive)</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">percent_rank (column_name)
  OVER ([[PARTITION BY grouping_column] [ORDER BY sorting_column]
        [RANGE BETWEEN UNBOUNDED PRECEDING AND UNBOUNDED FOLLOWING]] | [window_name])
FROM table_name
WINDOW window_name as ([PARTITION BY grouping_column] [ORDER BY sorting_column] RANGE BETWEEN UNBOUNDED PRECEDING AND UNBOUNDED FOLLOWING)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>The default and required window frame definition is <code>RANGE BETWEEN UNBOUNDED PRECEDING AND UNBOUNDED FOLLOWING</code>.</p><p>For more detail on window function syntax see: Window Functions - Syntax.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT player, salary,
       percent_rank() OVER (ORDER BY salary DESC) AS percent_rank
FROM (
    select c1::String as team, c2::String as player, c3::UInt32 as salary, c4::String as position from values (
      (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Gary Chen&#x27;, 195000, &#x27;F&#x27;),
      (&#x27;New Coreystad Archdukes&#x27;, &#x27;Charles Juarez&#x27;, 190000, &#x27;F&#x27;),
      (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Michael Stanley&#x27;, 150000, &#x27;D&#x27;),
      (&#x27;New Coreystad Archdukes&#x27;, &#x27;Scott Harrison&#x27;, 150000, &#x27;D&#x27;),
      (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Robert George&#x27;, 195000, &#x27;M&#x27;),
      (&#x27;South Hampton Seagulls&#x27;, &#x27;Douglas Benson&#x27;, 150000, &#x27;M&#x27;),
      (&#x27;South Hampton Seagulls&#x27;, &#x27;James Henderson&#x27;, 140000, &#x27;M&#x27;)
    )
)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─player──────────┬─salary─┬───────percent_rank─┐
│ Gary Chen       │ 195000 │                  0 │
│ Robert George   │ 195000 │                  0 │
│ Charles Juarez  │ 190000 │ 0.3333333333333333 │
│ Michael Stanley │ 150000 │                0.5 │
│ Scott Harrison  │ 150000 │                0.5 │
│ Douglas Benson  │ 150000 │                0.5 │
│ James Henderson │ 140000 │                  1 │
└─────────────────┴────────┴────────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="rank" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">rank<a class="headerlink" href="#rank" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Ranks the current row within its partition with gaps. In other words, if the value of any row it encounters is equal to the value of a previous row then it will receive the same rank as that previous row.<!-- --> <!-- -->The rank of the next row is then equal to the rank of the previous row plus a gap equal to the number of times the previous rank was given.</p><p>The dense_rank function provides the same behaviour but without gaps in ranking.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">rank (column_name)
  OVER ([[PARTITION BY grouping_column] [ORDER BY sorting_column]
        [ROWS or RANGE expression_to_bound_rows_withing_the_group]] | [window_name])
FROM table_name
WINDOW window_name as ([[PARTITION BY grouping_column] [ORDER BY sorting_column])
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>For more detail on window function syntax see: Window Functions - Syntax.</p><h3 id="returned-value" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returned value<a class="headerlink" href="#returned-value" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li>A number for the current row within its partition, including gaps. UInt64.</li></ul><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The following example is based on the example provided in the video instructional Ranking window functions in Tinybird.</p><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT player, salary,
       rank() OVER (ORDER BY salary DESC) AS rank
FROM (
    select c1::String as team, c2::String as player, c3::UInt32 as salary, c4::String as position from values (
      (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Gary Chen&#x27;, 195000, &#x27;F&#x27;),
      (&#x27;New Coreystad Archdukes&#x27;, &#x27;Charles Juarez&#x27;, 190000, &#x27;F&#x27;),
      (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Michael Stanley&#x27;, 150000, &#x27;D&#x27;),
      (&#x27;New Coreystad Archdukes&#x27;, &#x27;Scott Harrison&#x27;, 150000, &#x27;D&#x27;),
      (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Robert George&#x27;, 195000, &#x27;M&#x27;),
      (&#x27;South Hampton Seagulls&#x27;, &#x27;Douglas Benson&#x27;, 150000, &#x27;M&#x27;),
      (&#x27;South Hampton Seagulls&#x27;, &#x27;James Henderson&#x27;, 140000, &#x27;M&#x27;)
    )
)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─player──────────┬─salary─┬─rank─┐
│ Gary Chen       │ 195000 │    1 │
│ Robert George   │ 195000 │    1 │
│ Charles Juarez  │ 190000 │    3 │
│ Douglas Benson  │ 150000 │    4 │
│ Michael Stanley │ 150000 │    4 │
│ Scott Harrison  │ 150000 │    4 │
│ James Henderson │ 140000 │    7 │
└─────────────────┴────────┴──────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="row-number" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">row_number<a class="headerlink" href="#row-number" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Numbers the current row within its partition starting from 1.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">row_number (column_name)
  OVER ([[PARTITION BY grouping_column] [ORDER BY sorting_column]
        [ROWS or RANGE expression_to_bound_rows_withing_the_group]] | [window_name])
FROM table_name
WINDOW window_name as ([[PARTITION BY grouping_column] [ORDER BY sorting_column])
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>For more detail on window function syntax see: Window Functions - Syntax.</p><h3 id="returned-value" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returned value<a class="headerlink" href="#returned-value" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li>A number for the current row within its partition. UInt64.</li></ul><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The following example is based on the example provided in the video instructional Ranking window functions in Tinybird.</p><p>Query:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT player, salary,
       row_number() OVER (ORDER BY salary DESC) AS row_number
FROM (
    select c1::String as team, c2::String as player, c3::UInt32 as salary, c4::String as position from values (
      (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Gary Chen&#x27;, 195000, &#x27;F&#x27;),
      (&#x27;New Coreystad Archdukes&#x27;, &#x27;Charles Juarez&#x27;, 190000, &#x27;F&#x27;),
      (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Michael Stanley&#x27;, 150000, &#x27;D&#x27;),
      (&#x27;New Coreystad Archdukes&#x27;, &#x27;Scott Harrison&#x27;, 150000, &#x27;D&#x27;),
      (&#x27;Port Elizabeth Barbarians&#x27;, &#x27;Robert George&#x27;, 195000, &#x27;M&#x27;)
    )
)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─player──────────┬─salary─┬─row_number─┐
│ Gary Chen       │ 195000 │          1 │
│ Robert George   │ 195000 │          2 │
│ Charles Juarez  │ 190000 │          3 │
│ Michael Stanley │ 150000 │          4 │
│ Scott Harrison  │ 150000 │          5 │
└─────────────────┴────────┴────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></article><div class="flex items-center justify-end h-10" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><div class="italic text-caption"><span>Updated<!-- -->
